```{.python .input  n=1}
from keras.applications.mobilenet import MobileNet
from utils import load_keras_dataset
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
import numpy as np
from keras.utils.np_utils import to_categorical

from keras.layers import Input, Dense
from keras.models import Model
import keras
from patch._sklearn import get_learning_curve
from utils import (
    load_keras_dataset, concat_sample, batch_rescale
)

from utils import visualize_feature, down_sampling
from callbacks import FeedforwardHistory
from sklearn.decomposition import PCA

import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
plt.style.use('ggplot')
plt.ioff()
# plt.rcParams['font.family'] = 'Droid Sans Fallback'   # support zh-chinese
```


```{.python .input  n=2}
dataset_name = 'fashion_mnist'
(x_train, y_train), (x_test, y_test), (input_shape, num_classes) = load_keras_dataset(
    dataset_name, model_type='cnn'
)
```

```{.json .output n=2}
[
 {
  "name": "stdout",
  "output_type": "stream",
  "text": "x_train shape: (60000, 28, 28, 1)\ny_train shape: (60000,)\n60000 train samples\n10000 test samples\n"
 }
]
```

```{.python .input  n=3}
x_sub, y_sub = down_sampling(x_test, y_test)
x_sub_rescaled, input_shape = batch_rescale(x_sub, scale=4.56, to_3ch=True, to_generator=False)

print(input_shape)
print(x_sub_rescaled.shape)
```

```{.json .output n=3}
[
 {
  "name": "stdout",
  "output_type": "stream",
  "text": "(128, 128, 3)\n(1000, 128, 128, 3)\n"
 }
]
```

```{.python .input  n=4}
encoder = MobileNet(input_shape=input_shape, include_top=False,
                   weights='imagenet', pooling='max')

for l in encoder.layers: l.trainable = False
```

```{.python .input  n=5}
z = encoder.predict(x_sub_rescaled, batch_size=128)
pca = PCA(n_components=2, svd_solver='arpack').fit(z)
fig = visualize_feature(pca, z, y_sub, xlim=[-5, 5], ylim=[-5, 5], markersize=128)
display(fig)
```


```{.python .input  n=5}
h = Dense(512, activation='relu')(encoder.output)
yh = Dense(num_classes, activation='softmax')(h)

model = Model(encoder.input, yh)

model.compile(loss='categorical_crossentropy',
              optimizer='adam',
              metrics=['accuracy'])

latent_history = FeedforwardHistory(encoder, x_sub_rescaled, skip=10)

def make_batch_generator(x_gen, y_arr, input_shape, batch_size=128):
    x = np.zeros(tuple([batch_size] + list(input_shape)), dtype='float32')
    y = np.zeros(batch_size)
    _i = 0
    for _x, _y in zip(x_gen, y_arr):
        x[_i, :] = _x[0, :]
        y[_i] = _y        
        _i += 1   
        if _i == batch_size:
            _i = 0
            yield (x, to_categorical(y))
    
    yield (x[:_i, :], to_categorical(y[:_i]))
            
        
        
```

```{.python .input  n=7}
model.summary()
```

```{.python .input  n=6}
%%time
loops = 10
for _ in range(loops):
    x_train_rescaled, input_shape = batch_rescale(x_train, scale=4.56, to_3ch=True)
    history = model.fit_generator(
                    make_batch_generator(x_train_rescaled,
                                         y_train,
                                         input_shape,
                                         batch_size=256),
                    steps_per_epoch=40, epochs=5, verbose=1)
```
